## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Envoy HTTP Filter Chain Registration and Execution

## Your Task

Trace how HTTP filter chains are registered and executed in the Envoy proxy. Find C++ and protobuf files across envoyproxy/envoy and envoyproxy/data-plane-api that implement: the FilterChainFactory interface (in envoy/http/), the FilterChainHelper that constructs chains from config, the FilterManager that executes filter chains at runtime, and the HttpConnectionManager proto that defines the filter_chain configuration schema.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the crossrepo tracing domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/envoy--v1.31.2, sg-evals/data-plane-api--84e84367, sg-evals/go-control-plane--71637ad6, sg-evals/grpc--957dba5e.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/envoy--v1.31.2` (envoyproxy/envoy)
- `sg-evals/data-plane-api--84e84367` (envoyproxy/data-plane-api)
- `sg-evals/go-control-plane--71637ad6` (envoyproxy/go-control-plane)
- `sg-evals/grpc--957dba5e` (grpc/grpc)

## Summary of Findings

I've identified and documented **9 key files** that implement HTTP filter chain registration and execution:

### **Core Components:**

1. **FilterChainFactory Interface** (`envoy/http/filter_factory.h:89`)
   - Defines the contract for creating filter chains when new streams arrive

2. **FilterChainManager Interface** (`envoy/http/filter_factory.h:70`)
   - Abstract "sink" where filter factories are applied

3. **FilterManager** (`source/common/http/filter_manager.h:638`)
   - Concrete implementation that executes filters at runtime
   - Inherits from FilterChainManager
   - Manages decoder/encoder filter lists and iteration

4. **FilterChainHelper Template** (`source/common/http/filter_chain_helper.h:69`)
   - Processes HttpFilter protobuf configs during initialization
   - Creates FilterFactoryCb callbacks for each configured filter
   - Validates dependencies and handles dynamic configs

5. **HttpConnectionManagerConfig** (`source/extensions/filters/network/http_connection_manager/config.h:127`)
   - Main implementation of FilterChainFactory
   - Stores list of pre-created FilterFactoryCb
   - `createFilterChain()` method delegates to FilterChainUtility

6. **FilterChainUtility** (`source/common/http/filter_chain_helper.h:42`)
   - Static utility with `createFilterChainForFactories()` method
   - Iterates through factories and applies callbacks to FilterManager

7. **HttpConnectionManager Proto** (`envoy/extensions/filters/network/http_connection_manager/v3/http_connection_manager.proto:43`)
   - Contains `http_filters` repeated field defining the filter list

To do so, we compare the current latest with the *previous* filter. If they\\n37:   // match, then we must be processing a new filter for the first time. We omit this check if we're\\n38:   // the first filter, since the above check handles that case.\\n39:   //\\n40:   // We compare against the previous filter to avoid multiple filter iterations from resetting the\\n41:   // pointer: If we just set latest to current, then the first onData filter iteration would\\n42:   // correctly iterate over the filters and set latest, but on subsequent onData involves a clear separation between configuration-time registration (in `HttpConnectionManagerConfig`) and runtime execution (in `FilterManager`).\\n\\n## Core Components\\n\\n### 1. FilterChainFactory Interface (envoy/http/filter_factory.h, line 89)\\nThe `FilterChainFactory` interface defines the contract for creating filter chains:\\n- **createFilterChain()** - Called when a new HTTP stream is created on the connection. It receives a `FilterChainManager` where it applies filter factories.\\n- **createUpgradeFilterChain()** - Creates special filter chains for HTTP upgrade scenarios (e.g., WebSocket).\\n- Located in `envoy/http/filter_factory.h`\\n\\n### 2. FilterChainManager Interface (envoy/http/filter_factory.h, line 70)\\nThe `FilterChainManager` is the \\\"sink\\\" where filter factories are applied:\\n- **applyFilterFactoryCb()** - Applies a filter factory callback with contextual information.\\n- Implemented by `FilterManager` for actual stream-level execution.\\n\\n### 3. FilterFactoryCb Function Type (envoy/http/filter_factory.h, line 24)\\nA `FilterFactoryCb` is a function that creates filters for a specific stream:\\n```cpp\\nusing FilterFactoryCb = std::function<void(FilterChainFactoryCallbacks& callbacks)>;\\n```\\nEach filter factory receives callbacks to add decoder/encoder filters to the chain.\\n\\n### 4. FilterChainHelper Template (source/common/http/filter_chain_helper.h, line 69)\\nThe `FilterChainHelper` template processes HTTP filter configuration from protobuf:\\n- **processFilters()** - Iterates through HttpFilter proto configs and creates FilterFactoryCb for each.\\n- **processFilter()** - Processes a single HttpFilter config, looks up the registered factory, and creates a FilterFactoryCb.\\n- Handles static and dynamic filter configs.\\n- Validates filter dependencies.\\n- Used by `HttpConnectionManagerConfig` during initialization.\\n\\n### 5. FilterManager Implementation (source/common/http/filter_manager.h, line 638)\\nThe concrete `FilterManager` class executes filters at runtime:\\n- Inherits from `FilterChainManager` and `ScopeTrackedObject`.\\n- **applyFilterFactoryCb()** - Calls the factory callback to add filters to the stream.\\n- **decodeHeaders()** - Starts filter chain execution for request headers.\\n- **encodeHeaders()** - Starts filter chain execution for response headers.\\n- Maintains lists of decoder and encoder filters.\\n- Manages filter iteration and state tracking.\\n\\n### 6. HttpConnectionManagerConfig (source/extensions/filters/network/http_connection_manager/config.h, line 127)\\nThe main configuration class that implements `FilterChainFactory`:\\n- Processes HttpConnectionManager proto config during initialization.\\n- Stores `filter_factories_` - a list of `FilterFactoryCb` created by `FilterChainHelper`.\\n- **createFilterChain()** - Implementation at line 780-784 of config.cc:\\n  ```cpp\\n  bool HttpConnectionManagerConfig::createFilterChain(Http::FilterChainManager& manager, bool,\\n                                                      const Http::FilterChainOptions& options) const {\\n    Http::FilterChainUtility::createFilterChainForFactories(manager, options, filter_factories_);\\n    return true;\\n  }\\n  ```\\n- Creates the filter chain by delegating to `FilterChainUtility::createFilterChainForFactories`.\\n\\n### 7. FilterChainUtility (source/common/http/filter_chain_helper.h, line 42)\\nStatic utility methods for filter chain operations:\\n- **createFilterChainForFactories()** - Iterates through `FilterFactoriesList` and applies each factory callback to the manager, respecting filter disabled status and handling missing configs.\\n- Located in `source/common/http/filter_chain_helper.cc`.\\n\\n### 8. HttpConnectionManager Proto (envoy/extensions/filters/network/http_connection_manager/v3/http_connection_manager.proto, line 43)\\nProtobuf message defining HTTP connection manager configuration:\\n- **http_filters** field (line 471) - `repeated HttpFilter http_filters = 5;` - Defines the list of HTTP filters to be created for each stream.\\n- **upgrade_configs** field - Defines upgrade-specific filter chains.\\n- Other configuration fields like codec_type, stat_prefix, routing config, etc.\\n\\n### 9. HttpFilter Proto Message (envoy/extensions/filters/network/http_connection_manager/v3/http_connection_manager.proto, line 1339)\\nProtobuf message defining a single HTTP filter:\\n- Contains filter name and typed configuration.\\n- Supports both static and dynamic (via config_discovery) configurations.\\n- Can be marked as disabled or optional.\\n\\n## Execution Flow\\n\\n### Registration Phase (Configuration Time)\\n1. **HttpConnectionManager Filter Network Filter** receives the HttpConnectionManager proto config.\\n2. **HttpConnectionManagerConfig constructor** processes the config:\\n   - Uses `FilterChainHelper<Server::Configuration::FactoryContext, Server::Configuration::NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory>` to process `config.http_filters()`.\\n   - `FilterChainHelper::processFilters()` iterates through each HttpFilter proto.\\n   - For each filter, `FilterChainHelper::processFilter()` looks up the registered factory using `Config::Utility::getAndCheckFactory<NeutralNamedHttpFilterFactory>`.\\n   - Calls `factory->createFilterFactoryFromProto()` to create a `FilterFactoryCb`.\\n   - Stores these callbacks in a `FilterFactoriesList`.\\n3. **HttpConnectionManagerConfig stores** the list of `FilterFactoryCb` in `filter_factories_` member.\\n\\n### Execution Phase (Runtime)\\n1. **New HTTP stream arrives** at the connection (either from client or internally created).\\n2. **HttpConnectionManager** creates a new `FilterManager` and calls `filter_chain_factory_->createFilterChain(filter_manager_)`.\\n3. **HttpConnectionManagerConfig::createFilterChain()** is called:\\n   - Calls `FilterChainUtility::createFilterChainForFactories()` with the stored `filter_factories_`.\\n4. **FilterChainUtility::createFilterChainForFactories()** iterates through each `FilterFactoryCb`:\\n   - Checks if the filter is disabled (via route config or explicitly).\\n   - Calls the `FilterFactoryCb` function, passing the `FilterManager` as the `FilterChainFactoryCallbacks`.\\n   - Each callback adds decoder and/or encoder filters to the `FilterManager` using methods like `addStreamDecoderFilter()` and `addStreamEncoderFilter()`.\\n5. **FilterManager::decodeHeaders()** is called when request headers arrive:\\n   - Iterates through the decoder_filters_ list in order.\\n   - Calls each filter's `decodeHeaders()` method.\\n   - Continues until a filter stops iteration or all filters complete.\\n6. **Similar flow** for decode data, decode trailers, encode headers, encode data, and encode trailers.\\n7. **Filter execution** continues until the stream completes or terminates.\\n\\n## Key Design Patterns\\n\\n1. **Factory Pattern** - Factories create filters from proto configs, allowing flexible filter registration.\\n2. **Strategy Pattern** - Each filter implements the filter interface and can be swapped in/out.\\n3. **Chain of Responsibility** - Filters form a chain where each processes and potentially modifies data.\\n4. **Template Method** - `FilterChainHelper` uses templates to generalize filter processing for different contexts (downstream vs upstream).\\n5. **Separation of Concerns** - Configuration processing separated from runtime execution.\\n\\n## Configuration to Execution Mapping\\n\\n- **Proto Config** (HttpConnectionManager.http_filters) \u2192 **Factory Lookup** (Registry) \u2192 **FilterFactoryCb Creation** (factory->createFilterFactoryFromProto) \u2192 **Storage** (HttpConnectionManagerConfig.filter_factories_) \u2192 **Runtime Application** (FilterManager via applyFilterFactoryCb)\\n\"\n}\n",

involves a clear separation between configuration-time registration (in `HttpConnectionManagerConfig`) and runtime execution (in `FilterManager`).\\n\\n## Core Components\\n\\n### 1. FilterChainFactory Interface (envoy/http/filter_factory.h, line 89)\\nThe `FilterChainFactory` interface defines the contract for creating filter chains:\\n- **createFilterChain()** - Called when a new HTTP stream is created on the connection. It receives a `FilterChainManager` where it applies filter factories.\\n- **createUpgradeFilterChain()** - Creates special filter chains for HTTP upgrade scenarios (e.g., WebSocket).\\n- Located in `envoy/http/filter_factory.h`\\n\\n### 2. FilterChainManager Interface (envoy/http/filter_factory.h, line 70)\\nThe `FilterChainManager` is the \\\"sink\\\" where filter factories are applied:\\n- **applyFilterFactoryCb()** - Applies a filter factory callback with contextual information.\\n- Implemented by `FilterManager` for actual stream-level execution.\\n\\n### 3. FilterFactoryCb Function Type (envoy/http/filter_factory.h, line 24)\\nA `FilterFactoryCb` is a function that creates filters for a specific stream:\\n```cpp\\nusing FilterFactoryCb = std::function<void(FilterChainFactoryCallbacks& callbacks)>;\\n```\\nEach filter factory receives callbacks to add decoder/encoder filters to the chain.\\n\\n### 4. FilterChainHelper Template (source/common/http/filter_chain_helper.h, line 69)\\nThe `FilterChainHelper` template processes HTTP filter configuration from protobuf:\\n- **processFilters()** - Iterates through HttpFilter proto configs and creates FilterFactoryCb for each.\\n- **processFilter()** - Processes a single HttpFilter config, looks up the registered factory, and creates a FilterFactoryCb.\\n- Handles static and dynamic filter configs.\\n- Validates filter dependencies.\\n- Used by `HttpConnectionManagerConfig` during initialization.\\n\\n### 5. FilterManager Implementation (source/common/http/filter_manager.h, line 638)\\nThe concrete `FilterManager` class executes filters at runtime:\\n- Inherits from `FilterChainManager` and `ScopeTrackedObject`.\\n- **applyFilterFactoryCb()** - Calls the factory callback to add filters to the stream.\\n- **decodeHeaders()** - Starts filter chain execution for request headers.\\n- **encodeHeaders()** - Starts filter chain execution for response headers.\\n- Maintains lists of decoder and encoder filters.\\n- Manages filter iteration and state tracking.\\n\\n### 6. HttpConnectionManagerConfig (source/extensions/filters/network/http_connection_manager/config.h, line 127)\\nThe main configuration class that implements `FilterChainFactory`:\\n- Processes HttpConnectionManager proto config during initialization.\\n- Stores `filter_factories_` - a list of `FilterFactoryCb` created by `FilterChainHelper`.\\n- **createFilterChain()** - Implementation at line 780-784 of config.cc:\\n  ```cpp\\n  bool HttpConnectionManagerConfig::createFilterChain(Http::FilterChainManager& manager, bool,\\n                                                      const Http::FilterChainOptions& options) const {\\n    Http::FilterChainUtility::createFilterChainForFactories(manager, options, filter_factories_);\\n    return true;\\n  }\\n  ```\\n- Creates the filter chain by delegating to `FilterChainUtility::createFilterChainForFactories`.\\n\\n### 7. FilterChainUtility (source/common/http/filter_chain_helper.h, line 42)\\nStatic utility methods for filter chain operations:\\n- **createFilterChainForFactories()** - Iterates through `FilterFactoriesList` and applies each factory callback to the manager, respecting filter disabled status and handling missing configs.\\n- Located in `source/common/http/filter_chain_helper.cc`.\\n\\n### 8. HttpConnectionManager Proto (envoy/extensions/filters/network/http_connection_manager/v3/http_connection_manager.proto, line 43)\\nProtobuf message defining HTTP connection manager configuration:\\n- **http_filters** field (line 471) - `repeated HttpFilter http_filters = 5;` - Defines the list of HTTP filters to be created for each stream.\\n- **upgrade_configs** field - Defines upgrade-specific filter chains.\\n- Other configuration fields like codec_type, stat_prefix, routing config, etc.\\n\\n### 9. HttpFilter Proto Message (envoy/extensions/filters/network/http_connection_manager/v3/http_connection_manager.proto, line 1339)\\nProtobuf message defining a single HTTP filter:\\n- Contains filter name and typed configuration.\\n- Supports both static and dynamic (via config_discovery) configurations.\\n- Can be marked as disabled or optional.\\n\\n## Execution Flow\\n\\n### Registration Phase (Configuration Time)\\n1. **HttpConnectionManager Filter Network Filter** receives the HttpConnectionManager proto config.\\n2. **HttpConnectionManagerConfig constructor** processes the config:\\n   - Uses `FilterChainHelper<Server::Configuration::FactoryContext, Server::Configuration::NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory>` to process `config.http_filters()`.\\n   - `FilterChainHelper::processFilters()` iterates through each HttpFilter proto.\\n   - For each filter, `FilterChainHelper::processFilter()` looks up the registered factory using `Config::Utility::getAndCheckFactory<NeutralNamedHttpFilterFactory>`.\\n   - Calls `factory->createFilterFactoryFromProto()` to create a `FilterFactoryCb`.\\n   - Stores these callbacks in a `FilterFactoriesList`.\\n3. **HttpConnectionManagerConfig stores** the list of `FilterFactoryCb` in `filter_factories_` member.\\n\\n### Execution Phase (Runtime)\\n1. **New HTTP stream arrives** at the connection (either from client or internally created).\\n2. **HttpConnectionManager** creates a new `FilterManager` and calls `filter_chain_factory_->createFilterChain(filter_manager_)`.\\n3. **HttpConnectionManagerConfig::createFilterChain()** is called:\\n   - Calls `FilterChainUtility::createFilterChainForFactories()` with the stored `filter_factories_`.\\n4. **FilterChainUtility::createFilterChainForFactories()** iterates through each `FilterFactoryCb`:\\n   - Checks if the filter is disabled (via route config or explicitly).\\n   - Calls the `FilterFactoryCb` function, passing the `FilterManager` as the `FilterChainFactoryCallbacks`.\\n   - Each callback adds decoder and/or encoder filters to the `FilterManager` using methods like `addStreamDecoderFilter()` and `addStreamEncoderFilter()`.\\n5. **FilterManager::decodeHeaders()** is called when request headers arrive:\\n   - Iterates through the decoder_filters_ list in order.\\n   - Calls each filter's `decodeHeaders()` method.\\n   - Continues until a filter stops iteration or all filters complete.\\n6. **Similar flow** for decode data, decode trailers, encode headers, encode data, and encode trailers.\\n7. **Filter execution** continues until the stream completes or terminates.\\n\\n## Key Design Patterns\\n\\n1. **Factory Pattern** - Factories create filters from proto configs, allowing flexible filter registration.\\n2. **Strategy Pattern** - Each filter implements the filter interface and can be swapped in/out.\\n3. **Chain of Responsibility** - Filters form a chain where each processes and potentially modifies data.\\n4. **Template Method** - `FilterChainHelper` uses templates to generalize filter processing for different contexts (downstream vs upstream).\\n5. **Separation of Concerns** - Configuration processing separated from runtime execution.\\n\\n## Configuration to Execution Mapping\\n\\n- **Proto Config** (HttpConnectionManager.http_filters) \u2192 **Factory Lookup** (Registry) \u2192 **FilterFactoryCb Creation** (factory->createFilterFactoryFromProto) \u2192 **Storage** (HttpConnectionManagerConfig.filter_factories_) \u2192 **Runtime Application** (FilterManager via applyFilterFactoryCb)\\n\"\n}\n",
